(******************************************************************************************

 Subobjects in the category of partial setoids

 In this file, we characterize the internal logic of  the category of partial setoids in a
 first-order hyperdoctrine. To do so, we first give an alternative description of subobjects.
 Subobjects of a partial setoid `X` can equivalently be described as a formula `φ` in context
 [X] such that
 - if `φ [ x ]` holds, then also `x ~ x`
 - if both `x ~ y` and `φ [ x ]` hold, then so does `φ [ y ]`
 The first requirement expresses that everything that satisfies `φ`, also is a defined
 element, and the second requirement expresses that `φ` is well-defined with respect to the
 partial equivalence relation of `X`. This statement comes from Lemma 3.3 in "Tripos Theory
 in Retrospect" by Andrew Pitts.

 We also construct the displayed category of subobjects of partial setoids, and we show
 that this displayed category is univalent. In addition, we construct a cleaving on this
 displayed category, which gives us the substitution operation.

 References
 - "Tripos Theory in Retrospect" by Andrew Pitts

 Content
 1. Subobjects of partial setoids
 2. Accessors for subobjects of partial setoids
 3. Morphisms between subobjects of partial setoids
 4. The displayed category of subobjects
 5. This displayed category is univalent
 6. The cleaving

 ******************************************************************************************)

Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Hyperdoctrines.PartialEqRels.PERs.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Hyperdoctrines.PartialEqRels.PERMorphisms.

Local Open Scope cat.

Section PartialEqRelDispCat.
  Context {H : first_order_hyperdoctrine}.

  (** * 1. Subobjects of partial setoids *)
  Definition per_subobject_def_law
             {X : partial_setoid H}
             (φ : form X)
    : UU
    := let x := π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h X)) in
       (⊤ ⊢ ∀h (φ [ x ] ⇒ x ~ x)).

  Definition per_subobject_eq_law
             {X : partial_setoid H}
             (φ : form X)
    : UU
    := let x := π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h X))) in
       let y := π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h X)) in
       (⊤ ⊢ ∀h ∀h (x ~ y ⇒ φ [ x ] ⇒ φ [ y ])).

  Definition per_subobject_laws
             {X : partial_setoid H}
             (φ : form X)
    : UU
    := per_subobject_def_law φ
       ×
       per_subobject_eq_law φ.

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X: partial_setoid H
φ: form X
isaprop (per_subobject_laws φ)

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X: partial_setoid H
φ: form X
isaprop (per_subobject_laws φ)

    use isapropdirprod ;
      use invproofirrelevance ;
      intros p q ;
      apply hyperdoctrine_proof_eq.
  Qed.

  Definition per_subobject
             (X : partial_setoid H)
    : UU
    := ∑ (φ : form X), per_subobject_laws φ.

  Definition make_per_subobject
             {X : partial_setoid H}
             (φ : form X)
             (Hφ : per_subobject_laws φ)
    : per_subobject X
    := φ ,, Hφ.

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X: partial_setoid H
isaset (per_subobject X)

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X: partial_setoid H
isaset (per_subobject X)

    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X: partial_setoid H
isaset (form X)
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X: partial_setoid H
∏ x : form X, isaset (per_subobject_laws x)

    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X: partial_setoid H
isaset (form X)
 apply isaset_hyperdoctrine_formula.
    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X: partial_setoid H
∏ x : form X, isaset (per_subobject_laws x)
 
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X: partial_setoid H
ψ: form X
isaset (per_subobject_laws ψ)

      
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X: partial_setoid H
ψ: form X
isaprop (per_subobject_laws ψ)

      apply isaprop_per_subobject_laws.
  Qed.

  (** * 2. Accessors for subobjects of partial setoids *)
  Coercion per_subobject_to_form
           {X : partial_setoid H}
           (φ : per_subobject X)
    : form X
    := pr1 φ.

             [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h X)))]
             ⇒ (pr1 φ)
               [π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h X))])
          [⟨ ⟨ !! [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ]tm,
             π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ⟩
             [π₁ (tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h X)) ]tm,
           π₂ (tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h X)) ⟩]))

      π₂
        ((tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h X))
         [⟨ ⟨ tm_var Γ, x ⟩ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h X))
            ]tm, π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ⟩ ]tm)
      ⇒ (pr1 φ)
        [π₂
           ((π₁ (tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h X)))
            [⟨ ⟨ tm_var Γ, x ⟩
               [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ]tm,
             π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ⟩ ]tm)]
        ⇒ (pr1 φ)
          [π₂
             ((tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h X))
              [⟨ ⟨ tm_var Γ, x ⟩
                 [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ]tm,
               π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ⟩ ]tm)])
Δ ⊢ x ~ y ⇒ φ [x] ⇒ φ [y]

    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X: partial_setoid H
φ: per_subobject X
Γ: ty H
Δ: form Γ
x, y: tm Γ X
p₁: Δ ⊢ x ~ y
p₂: Δ ⊢ φ [x]
q': ⊤
⊢ ∀h (π₂
        (π₁
           ((tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h X))
            [⟨ ⟨ tm_var Γ, x ⟩
               [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ]tm,
             π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ⟩ ]tm)) ~
      π₂
        ((tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h X))
         [⟨ ⟨ tm_var Γ, x ⟩ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h X))
            ]tm, π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ⟩ ]tm)
      ⇒ (pr1 φ)
        [π₂
           (π₁
              ((tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h X))
               [⟨ ⟨ tm_var Γ, x ⟩
                  [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ]tm,
                π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ⟩ ]tm))]
        ⇒ (pr1 φ)
          [π₂
             ((tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h X))
              [⟨ ⟨ tm_var Γ, x ⟩
                 [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ]tm,
               π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ⟩ ]tm)])
Δ ⊢ x ~ y ⇒ φ [x] ⇒ φ [y]

  Qed.

  (** * 3. Morphisms between subobjects of partial setoids *)
  Definition per_subobject_mor_law
             {X Y : partial_setoid H}
             (φ : partial_setoid_morphism X Y)
             (ψ₁ : per_subobject X)
             (ψ₂ : per_subobject Y)
    : UU
    := let x := π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Y))) in
       let y := π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Y)) in
       (⊤ ⊢ ∀h ∀h (φ [ ⟨ x , y ⟩ ] ⇒ ψ₁ [ x ] ⇒ ψ₂ [ y ])).

  Arguments per_subobject_mor_law {X Y} φ ψ₁ ψ₂ /.

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X, Y: partial_setoid H
φ: partial_setoid_morphism X Y
ψ₁: per_subobject X
ψ₂: per_subobject Y
isaprop (per_subobject_mor_law φ ψ₁ ψ₂)

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X, Y: partial_setoid H
φ: partial_setoid_morphism X Y
ψ₁: per_subobject X
ψ₂: per_subobject Y
isaprop (per_subobject_mor_law φ ψ₁ ψ₂)

    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X, Y: partial_setoid H
φ: partial_setoid_morphism X Y
ψ₁: per_subobject X
ψ₂: per_subobject Y
isProofIrrelevant (per_subobject_mor_law φ ψ₁ ψ₂)

    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X, Y: partial_setoid H
φ: partial_setoid_morphism X Y
ψ₁: per_subobject X
ψ₂: per_subobject Y
p, q: per_subobject_mor_law φ ψ₁ ψ₂
p = q

    apply hyperdoctrine_proof_eq.
  Qed.

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X, Y: partial_setoid H
φ: partial_setoid_morphism X Y
ψ₁: per_subobject X
ψ₂: per_subobject Y
p: per_subobject_mor_law φ ψ₁ ψ₂
Γ: ty H
Δ: form Γ
x: tm Γ X
y: tm Γ Y
q₁: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ x, y ⟩]
q₂: Δ ⊢ ψ₁ [x]
Δ ⊢ ψ₂ [y]

  [!! : tm Γ 𝟙]

           [⟨ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Y))),
            π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Y)) ⟩])
          [⟨ ⟨ !! [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ]tm,
             π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ⟩
             [π₁ (tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h Y)) ]tm,
           π₂ (tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h Y)) ⟩]
          ⇒ (ψ₁ [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Y)))])
            [⟨ ⟨ !! [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ]tm,
               π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ⟩
               [π₁ (tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h Y)) ]tm,
             π₂ (tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h Y)) ⟩]
            ⇒ (ψ₂ [π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Y))])
              [⟨ ⟨ !! [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ]tm,
                 π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ⟩
                 [π₁ (tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h Y)) ]tm,
               π₂ (tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h Y)) ⟩]))
Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ x, y ⟩] ⇒ ψ₁ [x] ⇒ ψ₂ [y]

            [(π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)))
             [π₁ (tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h Y)) ]tm]
            ⇒ ψ₂ [π₂ (tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h Y))]))
Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ x, y ⟩] ⇒ ψ₁ [x] ⇒ ψ₂ [y]

    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine

r: ⊤

          [⟨ π₂
               ((tm_var (Γ ×h X))

           (π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Y)))
           [⟨ ⟨ (!! [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h X)) ]tm)
                [π₁ (tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h Y)) ]tm,
              π₂
                ((tm_var (Γ ×h X))
                 [π₁ (tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h Y)) ]tm)
              ⟩, π₂ (tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h Y)) ⟩ ]tm
           ⟩]
          ⇒ ψ₁
            [π₂
               ((tm_var (Γ ×h X))
                [π₁ (tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h Y)) ]tm)]
            ⇒ ψ₂ [π₂ (tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h Y))]))
Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ x, y ⟩] ⇒ ψ₁ [x] ⇒ ψ₂ [y]

              ((tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h Y))
               [⟨ ⟨ (tm_var Γ)
                    [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h Y)) ]tm,
                  x [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h Y)) ]tm ⟩,
                π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h Y)) ⟩ ]tm)),
       (π₂ (tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h Y)))
       [⟨ ⟨ (tm_var Γ) [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h Y)) ]tm,
          x [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h Y)) ]tm ⟩,
        π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h Y)) ⟩ ]tm ⟩]
      ⇒ ψ₁ [x [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h Y)) ]tm]
        ⇒ ψ₂ [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h Y))])
Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ x, y ⟩] ⇒ ψ₁ [x] ⇒ ψ₂ [y]

    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X, Y: partial_setoid H
φ: partial_setoid_morphism X Y
ψ₁: per_subobject X
ψ₂: per_subobject Y
p: per_subobject_mor_law φ ψ₁ ψ₂
Γ: ty H
Δ: form Γ
x: tm Γ X
y: tm Γ Y
q₁: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ x, y ⟩]
q₂: Δ ⊢ ψ₁ [x]
r': ⊤
⊢ ∀h (φ
      [⟨ π₂
           (π₁
              ⟨ ⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h Y)),
                x [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h Y)) ]tm ⟩,
              π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h Y)) ⟩),
       (π₂ (tm_var ((Γ ×h X) ×h Y)))
       [⟨ ⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h Y)),
          x [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h Y)) ]tm ⟩,
        π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h Y)) ⟩ ]tm ⟩]
      ⇒ ψ₁ [x [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h Y)) ]tm]
        ⇒ ψ₂ [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h Y))])
Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ x, y ⟩] ⇒ ψ₁ [x] ⇒ ψ₂ [y]

Δ ⊢ ⊤

    apply truth_intro.
  Qed.

  (** * 4. The displayed category of subobjects *)
  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
disp_cat_ob_mor (category_of_partial_setoids H)

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
disp_cat_ob_mor (category_of_partial_setoids H)

    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
category_of_partial_setoids H → UU
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
(λ obd : category_of_partial_setoids H → UU,
 ∏ x y : category_of_partial_setoids H,
 obd x
 → obd y → category_of_partial_setoids H ⟦ x, y ⟧ → UU)
  ?pr1

    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
category_of_partial_setoids H → UU
 exact (λ (X : partial_setoid H), per_subobject X).
    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
(λ obd : category_of_partial_setoids H → UU,
 ∏ x y : category_of_partial_setoids H,
 obd x
 → obd y → category_of_partial_setoids H ⟦ x, y ⟧ → UU)
  (λ X : partial_setoid H, per_subobject X)
 exact (λ (X Y : partial_setoid H)
               (ψ₁ : per_subobject X)
               (ψ₂ : per_subobject Y)
               (φ : partial_setoid_morphism X Y),
             per_subobject_mor_law φ ψ₁ ψ₂).
  Defined.

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
disp_cat_id_comp (category_of_partial_setoids H)
  disp_cat_ob_mor_per_subobject

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
disp_cat_id_comp (category_of_partial_setoids H)
  disp_cat_ob_mor_per_subobject

    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
∏ (x : category_of_partial_setoids H)
(xx : disp_cat_ob_mor_per_subobject x),
xx -->[ identity x] xx
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
∏ (x y z : category_of_partial_setoids H)
(f : category_of_partial_setoids H ⟦ x, y ⟧)
(g : category_of_partial_setoids H ⟦ y, z ⟧)
(xx : disp_cat_ob_mor_per_subobject x)
(yy : disp_cat_ob_mor_per_subobject y)
(zz : disp_cat_ob_mor_per_subobject z),
xx -->[ f] yy → yy -->[ g] zz → xx -->[ f · g] zz

    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
∏ (x : category_of_partial_setoids H)
(xx : disp_cat_ob_mor_per_subobject x),
xx -->[ identity x] xx

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
∏ (x y z : category_of_partial_setoids H)
(f : category_of_partial_setoids H ⟦ x, y ⟧)
(g : category_of_partial_setoids H ⟦ y, z ⟧)
(xx : disp_cat_ob_mor_per_subobject x)

xx -->[ f] yy → yy -->[ g] zz → xx -->[ f · g] zz
 
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X, Y, Z: category_of_partial_setoids H
φ₁: category_of_partial_setoids H ⟦ X, Y ⟧
φ₂: category_of_partial_setoids H ⟦ Y, Z ⟧
ψ₁: disp_cat_ob_mor_per_subobject X
ψ₂: disp_cat_ob_mor_per_subobject Y
ψ₃: disp_cat_ob_mor_per_subobject Z
p: ψ₁ -->[ φ₁] ψ₂
q: ψ₂ -->[ φ₂] ψ₃
ψ₁ -->[ φ₁ · φ₂] ψ₃

      
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X, Y, Z: partial_setoid H
φ₁: partial_setoid_morphism X Y
φ₂: partial_setoid_morphism Y Z
ψ₁: per_subobject X
ψ₂: per_subobject Y
ψ₃: per_subobject Z
p: per_subobject_mor_law φ₁ ψ₁ ψ₂
q: per_subobject_mor_law φ₂ ψ₂ ψ₃
⊤
⊢ ∀h (∀h ((∃h (φ₁
               [⟨ π₁ (π₁ (tm_var ((X ×h Z) ×h Y))),
                π₂ (tm_var ((X ×h Z) ×h Y)) ⟩]
               ∧ φ₂
                 [⟨ π₂ (tm_var ((X ×h Z) ×h Y)),
                  π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((X ×h Z) ×h Y))) ⟩]))
          [⟨ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Z))),
           π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Z)) ⟩]
          ⇒ ψ₁ [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Z)))]
            ⇒ ψ₃ [π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Z))]))

ψ₃: per_subobject Z
p: per_subobject_mor_law φ₁ ψ₁ ψ₂
q: per_subobject_mor_law φ₂ ψ₂ ψ₃
(⊤ [π₁ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h X))])
[π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Z))]

       ∧ φ₂

    [⟨ ⟨ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Z))),

φ₂: partial_setoid_morphism Y Z
ψ₁: per_subobject X
ψ₂: per_subobject Y
ψ₃: per_subobject Z
p: per_subobject_mor_law φ₁ ψ₁ ψ₂
q: per_subobject_mor_law φ₂ ψ₂ ψ₃
x:= π₂ (π₁ (π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Z) ×h Y)))): tm (((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Z) ×h Y) X
z:= π₂ (π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Z) ×h Y))): tm (((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Z) ×h Y) Z
(φ₁
 [⟨ π₁ (π₁ (tm_var ((X ×h Z) ×h Y))),
  π₂ (tm_var ((X ×h Z) ×h Y)) ⟩]
 ∧ φ₂
   [⟨ π₂ (tm_var ((X ×h Z) ×h Y)),
    π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((X ×h Z) ×h Y))) ⟩])
[⟨ ⟨ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Z))),
   π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Z)) ⟩
   [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Z) ×h Y)) ]tm,
 π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Z) ×h Y)) ⟩]
⊢ (ψ₁ [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Z)))])
  [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Z) ×h Y))]
  ⇒ (ψ₃ [π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Z))])
    [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h X) ×h Z) ×h Y))]

pq: z_iso_disp (identity_z_iso X) ψ₁ ψ₂
p:= pr1 pq: per_subobject_mor_law
  (id_partial_setoid_morphism X) ψ₁ ψ₂
q:= pr12 pq: per_subobject_mor_law
  (id_partial_setoid_morphism X) ψ₂ ψ₁
x:= tm_var X: tm X X
(pr1 ψ₂) [tm_var X] ⊢ ψ₂ [?x]

  (** * 6. The cleaving *)
  Section Substitution.
    Context {X Y : partial_setoid H}
            (φ : partial_setoid_morphism Y X)
            (ψ : per_subobject X).

    Let ζ : form Y
      := let y := π₁ (tm_var (Y ×h X)) in
         let x := π₂ (tm_var (Y ×h X)) in
         (∃h (φ [ ⟨ y , x ⟩ ] ∧ ψ [ x ])).

∧ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y))) ~
  π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y))
⊢ (∃h (φ
       [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Y ×h X)), π₂ (tm_var (Y ×h X)) ⟩]
       ∧ ψ [π₂ (tm_var (Y ×h X))]))
  [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y)))]
  ⇒ (∃h (φ
         [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Y ×h X)), π₂ (tm_var (Y ×h X))
          ⟩] ∧ ψ [π₂ (tm_var (Y ×h X))]))
    [π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y))]

y₂:= π₂ (π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y) ×h X))): tm (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y) ×h X) Y
x:= π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y) ×h X)): tm (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y) ×h X) X
y₁ ~ y₂ ∧ φ [⟨ y₁, x ⟩] ∧ ψ [x]
⊢ (φ
   [⟨ π₂
        (π₁
           (π₁ (tm_var ((((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X)))),
    π₂ (tm_var ((((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X)) ⟩]
   ∧ ψ [π₂ (tm_var ((((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X))])
  [⟨ tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y) ×h X), ?t ⟩]

y₁:= π₂ (π₁ (π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y) ×h X)))): tm (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y) ×h X) Y
y₂:= π₂ (π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y) ×h X))): tm (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y) ×h X) Y
x:= π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y) ×h X)): tm (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y) ×h X) X
φ [⟨ y₁, x ⟩] ∧ ψ [x] ⊢ φ [⟨ y₁, x ⟩]

x:= π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y) ×h X)): tm (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h Y) ×h X) X
φ [⟨ y₁, x ⟩] ⊢ φ [⟨ y₁, x ⟩]

               apply hyperdoctrine_hyp.

[⟨ π₂ (π₁ (π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X)))),
 π₂ (π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X))) ⟩]
∧ φ
  [⟨ π₂ (π₁ (π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X)))),
   π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X)) ⟩]
  ∧ ψ [π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X))]
⊢ ψ [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X)))]

      
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X, Y: partial_setoid H
φ: partial_setoid_morphism Y X
ψ: per_subobject X
ζ:= let y := π₁ (tm_var (Y ×h X)) in
let x := π₂ (tm_var (Y ×h X)) in
∃h (φ [⟨ y, x ⟩] ∧ ψ [x]): form Y
x₁:= π₂ (π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X))): tm (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X) X
x₂:= π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X)): tm (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X) X
y:= π₂ (π₁ (π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X)))): tm (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X) Y
φ
[⟨ π₂ (π₁ (π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X)))),
 π₂ (π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X))) ⟩]
∧ φ
  [⟨ π₂ (π₁ (π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X)))),
   π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X)) ⟩]
  ∧ ψ [π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X))]
⊢ ψ [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Y) ×h X) ×h X)))]

φ': partial_setoid_morphism W Y
ψ': per_subobject W
p: per_subobject_mor_law
  (partial_setoid_comp_morphism φ' φ) ψ' ψ
∃! gg : per_subobject_mor_law φ' ψ'
          (make_per_subobject ζ
             per_subobject_subst_laws),
(gg ;; per_subobject_subst_mor)%mor_disp = p

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine

W: partial_setoid H
φ': partial_setoid_morphism W Y
ψ': per_subobject W
p: per_subobject_mor_law
  (partial_setoid_comp_morphism φ' φ) ψ' ψ
isPredicate
  (λ x : per_subobject_mor_law φ' ψ'
           (make_per_subobject ζ
              per_subobject_subst_laws),
   (x ;; per_subobject_subst_mor)%mor_disp = p)
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
X, Y: partial_setoid H
φ: partial_setoid_morphism Y X
ψ: per_subobject X
ζ:= ∃h (φ
    [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Y ×h X)), π₂ (tm_var (Y ×h X)) ⟩]
    ∧ ψ [π₂ (tm_var (Y ×h X))]): form Y
W: partial_setoid H
φ': partial_setoid_morphism W Y
ψ': per_subobject W
p: per_subobject_mor_law
  (partial_setoid_comp_morphism φ' φ) ψ' ψ
∏
x
 y : per_subobject_mor_law φ' ψ'
       (make_per_subobject ζ per_subobject_subst_laws),
(λ x0 : per_subobject_mor_law φ' ψ'
          (make_per_subobject ζ
             per_subobject_subst_laws),
 (x0 ;; per_subobject_subst_mor)%mor_disp = p) x
→ (λ x0 : per_subobject_mor_law φ' ψ'
            (make_per_subobject ζ
               per_subobject_subst_laws),
   (x0 ;; per_subobject_subst_mor)%mor_disp = p) y
  → x = y

  [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h W) ×h Y) ×h X))]

  (partial_setoid_comp_morphism φ' φ) ψ' ψ
(φ'
 [⟨ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h W) ×h Y))),
  π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h W) ×h Y)) ⟩]

[π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h W) ×h Y) ×h X))]
∧ φ
  [⟨ (π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h W) ×h Y)))
     [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h W) ×h Y) ×h X)) ]tm,
   π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h W) ×h Y) ×h X)) ⟩]

        [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Y ×h X)), π₂ (tm_var (Y ×h X))
         ⟩] ∧ ψ [π₂ (tm_var (Y ×h X))]))
   [π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h W) ×h Y))])
  [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h W) ×h Y) ×h X))]

y:= π₂ (π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h W) ×h Y) ×h X))): tm (((𝟙 ×h W) ×h Y) ×h X) Y
x:= π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h W) ×h Y) ×h X)): tm (((𝟙 ×h W) ×h Y) ×h X) X
(φ' [⟨ w, y ⟩] ∧ ψ' [w]) ∧ φ [⟨ y, x ⟩] ⊢ ψ' [w]

    [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Y ×h X)), π₂ (tm_var (Y ×h X)) ⟩]
    ∧ ψ [π₂ (tm_var (Y ×h X))]): form Y

  (partial_setoid_comp_morphism φ' φ) ψ' ψ

               apply hyperdoctrine_hyp.
    Qed.
  End Substitution.
